# Comments for Question 4, LLM=o4-mini (medium reasoning)

== Grader: Claude 3.7 Sonnet ==
  * grade_story_10.txt (grade=7.5)
    The story effectively uses cooking as metaphor for emotional healing, with strong symbolic elements (recipes as family bonds, ingredients as memories). The central conflict between pride and forgiveness is clear, with a satisfying resolution. However, the story occasionally relies on telling emotional states rather than showing them, and some metaphors become repetitive. The theme of reconciliation is well-developed but could benefit from more subtlety.

  * grade_story_0.txt (grade=6.7)
    The story employs rich imagery and symbolism, particularly in how the lamp's fractured light represents the character's evolving hopes. However, the emotional impact is diluted by overly ornate language that sometimes prioritizes poetic description over narrative clarity. While there's a satisfying resolution in the monster's emergence and alliance, the story's thematic exploration of hope and forgotten oaths lacks sufficient grounding in concrete details to achieve its full potential.

  * grade_story_1.txt (grade=5.8)
    The story attempts literary depth through recurring motifs (knots/unraveling, boundaries/thresholds) and symbolic imagery, but relies too heavily on abstract language ("mundanely spiritual," "forbidden lore") rather than concrete specificity. While the central conflict of overcoming fear is present, the resolution lacks emotional weight due to insufficient character development. The theme of liberation through ancient knowledge emerges but remains underdeveloped beyond surface treatment.

  * grade_story_102.txt (grade=6.7)

  * grade_story_101.txt (grade=5.9)

  * grade_story_104.txt (grade=6.1)

Imagery is often striking (shadows dancing like specters). However, the theme feels overtly stated ("subversive hymn against uniformity," "lullaby of conformity") rather than emerging purely through subtext. The central conflict (steward vs. conformity) is present but lacks immediacy or significant stakes within the narrative's scope.

  * grade_story_100.txt (grade=6.0)

  * grade_story_0.txt (grade=4.8)
